<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a> (199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">findan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*finþaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pent-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go, pass; path, bridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">after searching</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plots.html>Plots</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vond.html>vond</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">All of a sudden I <b>found</b> a <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find, to think, to feel, to be of opinion

***vink.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vink.html>vink</a> (33692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinken.html>vinke</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*finkiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vink.html>vink</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinken.html>vinken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vink.html>vinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A chaffinch (<i>Fringilla coelebs</i>).</li>
<li>One of many other <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> of the family Fringillidae; a <a href = vnd.unilang:finch.html>finch</a>.</li>
<li>A Dutch dish that consists of pork and beef mince wrapped in bacon; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Short for <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">slavink</i></span></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A checkmark (often used in its diminutive form <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vink.html>vinkje</a>).</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Fringilla_coelebs" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Fringilla coelebs"><span style="color:green;"><i>Fringilla coelebs</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zangvogel.html>zangvogel</a></li>
<li>V-tje <a href = vnd.unilang:waarmee.html>waarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gecontroleerd.html>gecontroleerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:afvinken.html>afvinkt</a>'</li></ol>

***vinvis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinvis.html>vinvis</a> (58685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>17th century. Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vin.html>vin</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinvis.html>vinvis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinvis.html>vinvissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinvis.html>vinvisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any cetacean of the family Balaenopteridae, rorqual.</li>
<li>The fin whale, <i>Balaenoptera physalus</i>, in particular.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:viool.html>viool</a> (8810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">viole</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vitula</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:viool.html>viool</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:violen.html>violen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:viooltje.html>viooltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A violin, a popular musical string instrument of the soprano range.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">viole</i>, older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:violette.html>violette</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:violette.html>violette</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">viole</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:viola.html>viola</a></i>.
</p>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any <a href = vnd.unilang:violet.html>violet</a>, an ornamental fragrant plant of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:viola.html>Viola</a></i> (including the <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a>).

***vir.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a> (41335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">for; before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or rather the dialectal variant <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">veur</i> (compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a></i> vis-à-vis <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a></i>). The <a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a> distinction between <i class="Latn mention" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> may have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> influenced by corresponding <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">für</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>for</b> you!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Used to indicate the addressee of a communicative act.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:sy.html>Sy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roep.html>roep</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> sussie.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> calling <b>to</b> her little sister.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>Amen</a>, sê <a href = vnd.unilang:ek.html>ek</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:julle.html>julle</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>Amen</a>, I say <b>to</b> you.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> ou <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> gesein <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> motorbestuurder.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> signalled <b>to</b> the car driver.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Direct object marker.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrou.html>vrou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vir.html>vir</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inbreker.html>inbreker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> 'n <a href = vnd.unilang:hamer.html>hamer</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The woman then whacked the burglar with a hammer.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a> (1364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">visch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fisc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fiskaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pisḱ-</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">farmer, merchant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***vissen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a> (1617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">visschen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fiskon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fiskōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to fish, to try to catch fish</li>
<li>to fish (trying to get information)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***visser.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:visser.html>visser</a> (8809)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vischer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">visscher</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fiskar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fiskārijaz</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:visser.html>visser</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vissers.html>vissers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vissertje.html>vissertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">visster</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fisher, a fisherman or, less commonly, a fisherwoman.</li></ol>

***vit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vit.html>vit</a> (55533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*witją</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see, know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, archaic Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a></i>, akin to Old Saxon <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">giwit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>intelligence</li>
<li>consciousness
<ul><li><i>fáa <b>vitið</b> aftur</i>
<dl><dd>to regain consciousness</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vitamine.html>vitamine</a> (15876)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***vizier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>vizier</a> (7016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">visiere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">visiere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>vizier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>vizieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>viziertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>visor, a removable protective guard on a (knight's) helmet</li>
<li>backsight, a visual aiming aid on the barrel of a gun</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">visir</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">وزیر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vezir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">وَزِير</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">wazīr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">helper, aide, minister</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>vizier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>viziers</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>vizieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vizier.html>viziertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A high-ranking official or minister in an Islamic government, especially in the Ottoman Empire.</li></ol>

***vla.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vla.html>vla</a> (25522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vlade</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vlāde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*flatho</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*flatha</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*flaþō</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlaai.html>vlaai</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vla.html>vla</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vla.html>vla</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vla.html>vlaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sweet custard-based or cornflour-based <a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vla.html>vla</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoet.html>zoet</a> dikvloeibaar <a href = vnd.unilang:nagerecht.html>nagerecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> basis <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zuivel.html>zuivel</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vla.html>vla</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bord.html>bord</a> leegeten!</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vlage</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*flagōn-</i>, which could be related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fleuganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or otherwise to the root of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">flacor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flying, flickering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***vlaai.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlaai.html>vlaai</a> (62405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vlaeye</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vlaaye</i>, southeastern variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vlāde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*flado</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*flaþō</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vla.html>vla</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlaai.html>vlaai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlaaien.html>vlaaien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlaai.html>vlaaitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A type of fruit pie traditionally made and consumed in the Limburg province of the Netherlands.</li></ol>
